
    #############
    # By Lord R #
    #############

COM_clothes = {
	usage = game
	selection_behavior = weighted_random

    #Clothes for the Austrian Royals
    COM_AUS_royal_clothes = {
        dna_modifiers = {
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = com_military_coats
                template = com_AUS_noble_coats
                range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
            }
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = com_legwear
                template = com_AUS_legwear
                range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
            }
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = com_sashes
                template = com_AUS_sashes
                range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
            }
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = medals
                template = generic_medals
                range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
            }
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = belts
                template = all_belts
                range = { 0.1 0.7 } # For the randomness to work correctly
            }

            #Remove
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = coats
                template = no_coat
                range = { 0 0.27 } # limiting the set to single-breasted coats, so aiguillettes work
            }
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = aiguillettes
                template = no_aiguillettes
                range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
            }
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = epaulettes
                template = no_epaulette
                range = { 0 1 }
            }
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = top_layer
                template = no_top_layer
                range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
            }
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = legwear
                template = no_legwear
                range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
            }
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = headgear
                template = no_headgear
                range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
            }
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = sashes
                template = no_sash
                range = { 0 1 }
            }
        }
        weight = {
            base = 0
            modifier = {
                add = 500
                
                AND = {
                    exists = scope:character
                    scope:character = {
                        owner ?= {
                            OR = {
                                c:AUS ?= this
                                was_formed_from = AUS
                            }
                        }
                        monarchy_clothes_trigger = yes
                        is_female = no
                        age >= 13
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    #Clothes for the Baden Royals (early)
    COM_BAD_royal_clothes = {
        dna_modifiers = {
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = com_military_coats
                template = com_BAD_noble_coats
                range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
            }
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = com_legwear
                template = com_all_legwear
                accessory = male_legwear_european_01_black
            }
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = com_sashes
                template = com_BAD_sashes
                range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
            }
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = medals
                template = generic_medals
                range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
            }
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = belts
                template = all_belts
                range = { 0.1 0.7 } # For the randomness to work correctly
            }
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = com_epaulettes
                template = LUC_epaulettes
                range = { 0 1 }
            }

            #Remove
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = coats
                template = no_coat
                range = { 0 0.27 } # limiting the set to single-breasted coats, so aiguillettes work
            }
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = aiguillettes
                template = no_aiguillettes
                range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
            }
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = top_layer
                template = no_top_layer
                range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
            }
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = legwear
                template = no_legwear
                range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
            }
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = sashes
                template = no_sash
                range = { 0 1 }
            }
        }
        weight = {
            base = 0
            modifier = {
                add = 500
                
                AND = {
                    year < 1871
                    exists = scope:character
                    scope:character = {
                        owner ?= {
                            OR = {
                                c:BAD ?= this
                                was_formed_from = BAD
                            }
                        }
                        monarchy_clothes_trigger = yes
                        is_female = no
                        age >= 13
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

                template = no_epaulette
                range = { 0 1 }

                template = no_top_layer
                range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
            }
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = legwear
                template = no_legwear
                range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
            }
            accessory = {
                mode = add
                gene = sashes
                template = no_sash
                range = { 0 1 }
            }
        }
        weight = {
            base = 0
            modifier = {
                add = 500
                
                exists = scope:pop
                scope:pop = {
                    is_pop_type = soldiers
                    exists = home_country
                    OR = {
                        home_country = {
                            was_formed_from = GRE
                        }
                        AND = {
                            exists = c:GRE
                            home_country = c:GRE
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                add = 300

                scope:pop = {
                    is_pop_type = soldiers
                    AND = {
                        exists = home_country
                        home_country = {
                            country_has_primary_culture = cu:greek
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
